msg:Nanjing is a city worth visiting. It was a wise choice to choose Xuanwu Lake Holiday Inn for this stay.
1 It is very close to several attractions we want to visit: Hongshan Forest Zoo (about 3km), Zhongshan Scenic Area (Ming Xiaoling Mausoleum, Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, Meiling Palace, Music Stage, Linggu Temple) Didi is about 10 yuan, Xuanwu Lake (cross the street from the hotel is Jinling Style Square, and across the square is Xuanwu Lake) and Nanjing Railway Station are also very close. We drove by ourselves. We walked straight out of the hotel and got on the highway (frame) very quickly.
2 The subway is very convenient. Turn left and you will see the subway station, Gangzi Village on Line 4. It takes 2 stops to Jiming Temple. From Jiming Temple, transfer to Line 3 and 4 stops to Confucius Temple Qinhuai River.
3 Opposite the hotel is Jinling Style Square, which has all kinds of food. We ate Nanjing food stalls, Zhuangyuan Jidi, and drank Luckin Coffee.
4 The hotel service is very good. A few details, upgraded to a lake view room with a balcony, facing Xuanwu Lake, the scenery is so beautiful that there is nothing to say, the staff are smiling when talking (including the waitress who makes noodles for breakfast, she is sweating, but still smiling, very beautiful and elegant), the front desk handed over the room card with both hands, we usually drink a lot of water, bought a box of water and put it in the car, and brought it back to the hotel every day. The waiter probably saw that we had 8 or 9 bottles of mineral water bottles in the trash can every day, so he put 4 bottles of water for us every day (of course, I don‚Äôt know if every room is like this), although it would be no problem if we went to the front desk to ask for a few more bottles of water, but such details make people feel comfortable.
5. Convenient parking, there are many underground parking spaces, free. It‚Äôs just that it‚Äôs not convenient to go to the front desk every time you go out. It would be great if this step could be avoided.
6. Knowing that you are a member, you can also send a member drink coupon, and a thoughtful reminder, if you need it, you can go to the front desk to let us know.
7. Finally, the hotel‚Äôs food, rich breakfast, all kinds of them, and Nanjing‚Äôs special duck blood vermicelli soup, very delicious. (The coffee machine is a bit slow, so I'll adjust it quickly.) In addition, the hotel has a buffet on Friday and Saturday nights. We checked in on Friday and Saturday, so we ate there once. The price-performance ratio is super high. The buffet that costs 138 on Dianping.com is only 104 for hotel guests. There are lamb chops, barbecue, spicy hot pot, crayfish, roast duck, various drinks and alcohol, and other things (basically everything). I even saw... live pearls. Although I didn't eat them, it was the first time I saw them. I was shocked, haha. Friends who like to eat should be satisfied.
In short, the experience is very good. I will choose to stay here next time I travel to Nanjing.
